97→\tv.SetEnvKeyReplacer(strings.NewReplacer(\".\", \"_\"))\n    98→\tv.AutomaticEnv()\n    99→\n   100→\tvar cfg *Config\n   101→\n   102→\tif path == \"\" {\n   103→\t\tcfg = Default()\n   104→\t} else {\n   105→\t\tcfg = &Config{}\n   106→\t\tfile, err := getConfigFile(ctx, path)\n   107→\t\tif err != nil {\n   108→\t\t\treturn nil, err\n   109→\t\t}\n   110→\t\tdefer file.Close()\n   111→\t\tstat, err := file.Stat()\n   112→\t\tif err != nil {\n   113→\t\t\treturn nil, err\n   114→\t\t}\n   115→\n   116→\t\t// reimplement logic from v.ReadInConfig()\n   117→\t\tv.SetConfigFile(stat.Name())\n   118→\t\text := filepath.Ext(stat.Name())\n   119→\t\tif len(ext) > 1 {\n   120→\t\t\text = ext[1:]\n   121→\t\t}\n   122→\t\tif !slices.Contains(viper.SupportedExts, ext) {\n   123→\t\t\treturn nil, viper.UnsupportedConfigError(ext)\n   124→\t\t}\n   125→\t\tif err := v.ReadConfig(file); err != nil {\n   126→\t\t\treturn nil, err\n   127→\t\t}\n   128→\n   129→\t\t// This is a fix for issue #4428. By default, Viper uses lowercase keys and the allowed_teams with case-sensitive keys\n   130→\t\t// will be converted to lowercase. This will cause issues when matching against allowed_organizations. This workaround\n   131→\t\t// tries to restore the original case of the keys in allowed_teams if they match any of the allowed_organizations.\n   132→\t\tif v.IsSet(\"authentication.methods.github.allowed_teams\") && v.IsSet(\"authentication.methods.github.allowed_organizations\") {\n   133→\t\t\tallowedTeams := v.GetStringMapStringSlice(\"authentication.methods.github.allowed_teams\")\n   134→\t\t\torgs := (v.GetStringSlice(\"authentication.methods.github.allowed_organizations\"))\n   135→\t\t\tfor org, teams := range allowedTeams {\n   136→\t\t\t\tif slices.Contains(orgs, org) {\n   137→\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n   138→\t\t\t\t}\n   139→\n   140→\t\t\t\tif i := slices.IndexFunc(orgs, func(o string) bool {\n   141→\t\t\t\t\treturn org == strings.ToLower(o)\n   142→\t\t\t\t}); i != -1 {\n   143→\t\t\t\t\tdelete(allowedTeams, org)\n   144→\t\t\t\t\tallowedTeams[orgs[i]] = teams\n   145→\t\t\t\t}\n   146→\n   147→\t\t\t}\n   148→\t\t\tv.Set(\"authentication.methods.github.allowed_teams\", allowedTeams)\n   149→\t\t}\n   150→\t}\n   151→\n   152→\tvar (\n   153→\t\tresult      = &Result{Config: cfg}\n   154→\t\tdeprecators []deprecator\n   155→\t\tdefaulters  []defaulter\n   156→\t\tvalidators  []validator\n   157→\t)\n   158→\n   159→\tf := func(field any) {\n   160→\t\t// for-each deprecator implementing field we collect\n   161→\t\t// them up and return them to be run before unmarshalling and before setting defaults.\n   162→\t\tif deprecator, ok := field.(deprecator); ok {\n   163→\t\t\tdeprecators = append(deprecators, deprecator)\n   164→\t\t}\n   165→\n   166→\t\t// for-each defaulter implementing fields we invoke\n   167→\t\t// setting any defaults during this prepare stage\n   168→\t\t// on the supplied viper.\n   169→\t\tif defaulter, ok := field.(defaulter); ok {\n   170→\t\t\tdefaulters = append(defaulters, defaulter)\n   171→\t\t}\n   172→\n   173→\t\t// for-each validator implementing field we collect\n   174→\t\t// them up and return them to be validated after\n   175→\t\t// unmarshalling.\n   176→\t\tif validator, ok := field.(validator); ok {\n   177→\t\t\tvalidators = append(validators, validator)\n   178→\t\t}\n   179→\t}\n   180→\n   181→\t// invoke the field visitor on the root config firsts\n   182→\troot := reflect.ValueOf(cfg).Interface()\n   183→\tf(root)\n   184→\n   185→\t// these are reflected config top-level types for fields where\n   186→\t// they have been marked as experimental and their associated\n   187→\t// flag has enabled set to false.\n   188→\tvar skippedTypes []reflect.Type\n   189→\n   190→\tval := reflect.ValueOf(cfg).Elem()\n   191→\tfor i := range val.NumField() {\n   192→\t\t// search for all expected env vars since Viper cannot\n   193→\t\t// infer when doing Unmarshal + AutomaticEnv.\n   194→\t\t// see: https://github.com/spf13/viper/issues/761\n   195→\t\tstructField := val.Type().Field(i)\n   196→\t\tif exp := structField.Tag.Get(\"experiment\"); exp != \"\" {\n   197→\t\t\tif !v.GetBool(fmt.Sprintf(\"experimental.%s.enabled\", exp)) {\n   198→\t\t\t\tskippedTypes = append(skippedTypes, structField.Type)\n   199→\t\t\t}\n   200→\t\t}\n   201→\n   202→\t\tkey := fieldKey(structField)\n   203→\t\tbindEnvVars(v, getFliptEnvs(), []string{key}, structField.Type)\n   204→\n   205→\t\tfield := val.Field(i).Addr().Interface()\n   206→\t\tf(field)\n   207→\t}\n   208→\n   209→\t// run any deprecations checks\n   210→\tfor _, deprecator := range deprecators {\n   211→\t\twarnings := deprecator.deprecations(v)\n   212→\t\tfor _, warning := range warnings {\n   213→\t\t\tresult.Warnings = append(result.Warnings, warning.Message())\n   214→\t\t}\n   215→\t}\n   216→\n   217→\t// run any defaulters\n   218→\tfor _, defaulter := range defaulters {\n   219→\t\tif err := defaulter.setDefaults(v); err != nil {\n   220→\t\t\treturn nil, err\n   221→\t\t}\n   222→\t}\n   223→\n   224→\tif err := v.Unmarshal(cfg, viper.DecodeHook(\n   225→\t\tmapstructure.ComposeDecodeHookFunc(\n   226→\t\t\tappend(DecodeHooks, experimentalFieldSkipHookFunc(skippedTypes...))...,\n   227→\t\t),\n   228→\t)); err != nil {\n   229→\t\treturn nil, err\n   230→\t}\n   231→\n   232→\t// run any validation steps\n   233→\tfor _, validator := range validators {\n   234→\t\tif err := validator.validate(); err != nil {\n   235→\t\t\treturn nil, err\n   236→\t\t}\n   237→\t}\n   238→\n   239→\treturn result, nil\n   240→}\n   241→\n   242→// getConfigFile provides a file from different types of storage.\n   243→func getConfigFile(ctx context.Context, path string) (fs.File, error) {\n   244→\tu, err := url.Parse(path)\n   245→\tif err != nil {\n   246→\t\treturn nil, err\n   247→\t}\n   248→\n   249→\tif slices.Contains(object.SupportedSchemes(), u.Scheme) {\n   250→\t\tkey := strings.TrimPrefix(u.Path, \"/\")\n   251→\t\tu.Path = \"\"\n   252→\t\tbucket, err := object.OpenBucket(ctx, u)\n   253→\t\tif err != nil {\n   254→\t\t\treturn nil, err\n   255→\t\t}\n   256→\t\tdefer bucket.Close()\n   257→\t\tbucket.SetIOFSCallback(func() (context.Context, *blob.ReaderOptions) { return ctx, nil })\n   258→\t\treturn bucket.Open(key)\n   259→\t}\n   260→\n   261→\t// assumes that the local file is used\n   262→\tfile, err := os.Open(path)\n   263→\tif err != nil {\n   264→\t\treturn nil, err\n   265→\t}\n   266→\treturn file, nil\n   267→}\n   268→\n   269→type defaulter interface {\n   270→\tsetDefaults(v *viper.Viper) error\n   271→}\n   272→\n   273→type validator interface {\n   274→\tvalidate() error\n   275→}\n   276→\n   277→type deprecator interface {\n   278→\tdeprecations(v *viper.Viper) []deprecated\n   279→}\n   280→\n   281→// fieldKey returns the name to be used when deriving a fields env var key.\n   282→// If marked as squash the key will be the empty string.\n   283→// Otherwise, it is derived from the lowercase name of the field.\n   284→func fieldKey(field reflect.StructField) string {\n   285→\tif tag := field.Tag.Get(\"mapstructure\"); tag != \"\" {\n   286→\t\ttag, attr, ok := strings.Cut(tag, \",\")\n   287→\t\tif !ok || attr == \"squash\" || attr == \"omitempty\" {\n   288→\t\t\treturn tag\n   289→\t\t}\n   290→\t}\n   291→\n   292→\treturn strings.ToLower(field.Name)\n   293→}\n   294→\n   295→type envBinder interface {\n   296→\tMustBindEnv(...string)\n   297→}\n   298→\n   299→// bindEnvVars descends into the provided struct field binding any expected\n   300→// environment variable keys it finds reflecting struct and field tags.\n   301→func bindEnvVars(v envBinder, env, prefixes []string, typ reflect.Type) {\n   302→\t// descend through pointers\n   303→\tif typ.Kind() == reflect.Pointer {\n   304→\t\ttyp = typ.Elem()\n   305→\t}\n   306→\n   307→\tswitch typ.Kind() {\n   308→\tcase reflect.Map:\n   309→\t\t// recurse into bindEnvVars while signifying that the last\n   310→\t\t// key was unbound using the wildcard \"*\".\n   311→\t\tbindEnvVars(v, env, append(prefixes, wildcard), typ.Elem())\n   312→\n   313→\t\treturn\n   314→\tcase reflect.Struct, reflect.Slice:\n   315→\t\tif typ.Kind() == reflect.Slice {\n   316→\t\t\tif typ = typ.Elem(); typ.Kind() != reflect.Struct {\n   317→\t\t\t\tbreak\n   318→\t\t\t}\n   319→\t\t}\n   320→\n   321→\t\tfor structField := range typ.Fields() {\n   322→\t\t\tkey := fieldKey(structField)\n   323→\n   324→\t\t\tbind(env, prefixes, key, func(prefixes []string) {\n   325→\t\t\t\tbindEnvVars(v, env, prefixes, structField.Type)\n   326→\t\t\t})\n   327→\t\t}\n   328→\n   329→\t\treturn\n   330→\t}\n   331→\n   332→\tbind(env, prefixes, \"\", func(prefixes []string) {\n   333→\t\tv.MustBindEnv(strings.Join(prefixes, \".\"))\n   334→\t})\n   335→}\n   336→\n   337→const wildcard = \"*\"\n   338→\n   339→func appendIfNotEmpty(s []string, v ...string) []string {\n   340→\tfor _, vs := range v {\n   341→\t\tif vs != \"\" {\n   342→\t\t\ts = append(s, vs)\n   343→\t\t}\n   344→\t}\n   345→\n   346→\treturn s\n   347→}\n   348→\n   349→// bind invokes the supplied function \"fn\" with each possible set of\n   350→// prefixes for the next prefix (\"next\").\n   351→// If the last prefix is \"*\" then we must search the current environment\n   352→// for matching env vars to obtain the potential keys which populate\n   353→// the unbound map keys.\n   354→func bind(env, prefixes []string, next string, fn func([]string)) {\n   355→\t// given the previous entry is non-existent or not the wildcard\n   356→\tif len(prefixes) < 1 || prefixes[len(prefixes)-1] != wildcard {\n   357→\t\tfn(appendIfNotEmpty(prefixes, next))\n   358→\t\treturn\n   359→\t}\n   360→\n   361→\t// drop the wildcard and derive all the possible keys from\n   362→\t// existing environment variables.\n   363→\tp := make([]string, len(prefixes)-1)\n   364→\tcopy(p, prefixes[:len(prefixes)-1])\n   365→\n   366→\tvar (\n   367→\t\t// makezero linter doesn't take note of subsequent copy\n   368→\t\t// nolint https://github.com/ashanbrown/makezero/issues/12\n   369→\t\tprefix = strings.ToUpper(strings.Join(append(p, \"\"), \"_\"))\n   370→\t\tkeys   = strippedKeys(env, prefix, strings.ToUpper(next))\n   371→\t)\n   372→\n   373→\tfor _, key := range keys {\n   374→\t\tfn(appendIfNotEmpty(p, strings.ToLower(key), next))\n   375→\t}\n   376→}\n   377→\n   378→// strippedKeys returns a set of keys derived from a list of env var keys.\n   379→// It starts by filtering and stripping each key with a matching prefix.\n   380→// Given a child delimiter string is supplied it also trims the delimeter string\n   381→// and any remaining characters after this suffix.\n   382→//\n   383→// e.g strippedKeys([\"A_B_C_D\", \"A_B_F_D\", \"A_B_E_D_G\"], \"A_B\", \"D\")\n   384→// returns [\"c\", \"f\", \"e\"]\n   385→//\n   386→// It's purpose is to extract the parts of env vars which are likely\n   387→// keys in an arbitrary map type.\n   388→func strippedKeys(envs []string, prefix, delim string) (keys []string) {\n   389→\tfor _, env := range envs {\n   390→\t\tif strings.HasPrefix(env, prefix) {\n   391→\t\t\tenv = env[len(prefix):]\n   392→\t\t\tif env == \"\" {\n   393→\t\t\t\tcontinue\n   394→\t\t\t}\n   395→\n   396→\t\t\tif delim == \"\" {\n   397→\t\t\t\tkeys = append(keys, env)\n   398→\t\t\t\tcontinue\n   399→\t\t\t}\n   400→\n   401→\t\t\t// cut the string on the child key and take the left hand component\n   402→\t\t\tif left, _, ok := strings.Cut(env, \"_\"+delim); ok {\n   403→\t\t\t\tkeys = append(keys, left)\n   404→\t\t\t}\n   405→\t\t}\n   406→\t}\n   407→\treturn\n   408→}\n   409→\n   410→// getFliptEnvs returns all environment variables which have FLIPT_\n   411→// as a prefix. It also strips this prefix before appending them to the\n   412→// resulting set.\n   413→func getFliptEnvs() (envs []string) {\n   414→\tconst prefix = \"FLIPT_\"\n   415→\tfor _, e := range os.Environ() {\n   416→\t\tkey, _, ok := strings.Cut(e, \"=\")\n   417→\t\tif ok && strings.HasPrefix(key, prefix) {\n   418→\t\t\t// strip FLIPT_ off env vars for convenience\n   419→\t\t\tenvs = append(envs, key[len(prefix):])\n   420→\t\t}\n   421→\t}\n   422→\treturn envs\n   423→}\n   424→\n   425→func (c *Config) validate() error {\n   426→\tif c.Version != \"\" {\n   427→\t\tif strings.TrimSpace(c.Version) != Version {\n   428→\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"invalid version: %s\", c.Version)\n   429→\t\t}\n   430→\t}\n   431→\n   432→\tif c.Authorization.Required && !c.Authentication.Required {\n   433→\t\treturn errString(\"authorization\", \"requires authentication to also be required\")\n   434→\t}\n   435→\n   436→\t// Check that environment storage references exist in storage config\n   437→\tfor envName, env := range c.Environments {\n   438→\t\tif env.Storage == \"\" {\n   439→\t\t\tcontinue\n   440→\t\t}\n   441→\n   442→\t\tif _, exists := c.Storage[env.Storage]; !exists {\n   443→\t\t\treturn errString(\"environments\", fmt.Sprintf(\"%q references undefined storage %q\", envName, env.Storage))\n   444→\t\t}\n   445→\t}\n   446→\n   447→\t// Validate templates config\n   448→\tif err := c.Templates.Validate(); err != nil {\n   449→\t\treturn errFieldWrap(\"\", \"templates\", err)\n   450→\t}\n   451→\n   452→\treturn nil\n   453→}\n   454→\n   455→func (c *Config) ServeHTTP(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n   456→\tvar (\n   457→\t\tout []byte\n   458→\t\terr error\n   459→\t)\n   460→\n   461→\tif 473→\t\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusInternalServerError)\n   474→\t\treturn\n   475→\t}\n   476→}\n   477→\n   478→// stringToEnumHookFunc returns a DecodeHookFunc that converts strings to a target enum\n   479→func stringToEnumHookFunc[T constraints.Integer](mappings map[string]T) mapstructure.DecodeHookFunc {\n   480→\treturn func(\n   481→\t\tf reflect.Type,\n   482→\t\tt reflect.Type,\n   483→\t\tdata any,\n   484→\t) (any, error) {\n   485→\t\tif f.Kind() != reflect.String {\n   486→\t\t\treturn data, nil\n   487→\t\t}\n   488→\t\tif t != reflect.TypeOf(T(0)) {\n   489→\t\t\treturn ...reflect.Type) mapstructure.DecodeHookFunc {\n   499→\treturn func(\n   500→\t\tf reflect.Type,\n   501→\t\tt reflect.Type,\n   502→\t\tdata any,\n   503→\t) (any, error) {\n   504→\t\tif len(types) == 0 {\n   505→\t\t\treturn data, nil\n   506→\t\t}\n   507→\n   508→\t\tif t.Kind() != reflect.Struct {\n   509→\t\t\treturn data, nil\n   510→\t\t}\n   511→\n   512→\t\t// skip any types that match a type in the provided set\n   513→\t\tfor _, typ := range types {\n   514→\t\t\tif t == typ {\n   515→\t\t\t\treturn reflect.New(typ).Interface(), nil\n   516→\t\t\t}\n   517→\t\t}\n   518→\n   519→\t\treturn data, nil\n   520→\t}\n   521→}\n   522→\n   523→// stringToReferenceHookFunc returns a DecodeHookFunc that handles:\n   524→// - ${env:VAR} - environment variables\n   525→// - ${secret:key} - secret references (marked as unresolved placeholders)\n   526→func stringToReferenceHookFunc() mapstructure.DecodeHookFunc {\n   527→\treturn func(\n   528→\t\tf reflect.Type,\n   529→\t\tt reflect.Type,\n   530→\t\tdata any,\n   531→\t) (any, error) {\n   532→\t\tif f.Kind() != reflect.String || f != reflect.TypeFor[string]() {\n   533→\t\t\treturn data, nil\n   534→\t\t}\n   535→\n   536→\t\tstr := data.(string)\n   537→\n   538→\t\t// Handle explicit environment references: ${env:VAR}\n   539→\t\tif envReference.MatchString(str) {\n   540→\t\t\tkey := 545→\t\treturn data, nil\n   546→\t}\n   547→}\n   548→\n   549→// stringToSliceHookFunc returns a DecodeHookFunc that converts\n   550→// string to []string by splitting using strings.Fields().\n   551→func stringToSliceHookFunc() mapstructure.DecodeHookFunc {\n   552→\treturn func(\n   553→\t\tf reflect.Kind,\n   554→\t\tt reflect.Kind,\n   555→\t\tdata any,\n   556→\t) (any, error) {\n   557→\t\tif f != reflect.String || t != reflect.Slice {\n   558→\t\t\treturn data, nil\n   559→\t\t}\n   560→\n   561→\t\traw := data.(string)\n   562→\t\tif raw == \"\" {\n   563→\t\t\treturn provided.\n   571→func Default() *Config {\n   572→\treturn &Config{\n   573→\t\tLog: LogConfig{\n   574→\t\t\tLevel:     \"INFO\",\n   575→\t\t\tEncoding:  LogEncodingConsole,\n vars to obtain the potential keys which populate\n// the unbound map keys.\nfunc bind(env, prefixes []string, next string, fn func([]string)) {\n\t// given the previous entry is non-existent or not keys.\n// It starts by filtering and stripping each key with a matching prefix.\n// Given a child delimiter string is supplied it also trims the delimeter string\n// and any remaining characters after this suffix.\n//\n// e.g strippedKeys([\"A_B_C_D\", \"A_B_F_D\", \"A_B_E_D_G\"], \"A_B\", \"D\")\n// returns [\"c\", \"f\", \"e\"]\n//\n// It's purpose is to extract the parts of env vars which are likely\n// keys in an arbitrary map type.\nfunc strippedKeys(envs []string, prefix, delim string) (keys []string) {\n\tfor _, env := range envs {\n\t\tif strings.HasPrefix(env, prefix) {\n\t\t\tenv = env[len(prefix):]\n\t\t\tif env == \"\" {\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tif delim == \"\" {\n\t\t\t\tkeys = append(keys, env)\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t// cut the string on the child key and take the left hand component\n\t\t\tif left, _, ok := strings.Cut(env, \"_\"+delim); ok {\n\t\t\t\tkeys = append(keys, left)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn\n}\n\n// getFliptEnvs returns all environment variables which have FLIPT_\n// as a prefix. values and builds up a set of environment variables\n// compatible with viper's expectations for automatic env capability.\nfunc readYAMLIntoEnv(t *testing.T, path string) [][2]string {\n\tt.Helper()\n\n\tconfigFile, err := os.ReadFile(path)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\tvar config map[any]any\n\terr = yaml.Unmarshal(configFile, &config)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\treturn getEnvVars(\"flipt\", config)\n}\n\nfunc getEnvVars(prefix string, v map[any]any) (vals [][2]string) {\nOUTER:\n\tfor key, value := range v {\n\t\tswitch v := value.(type) {\n\t\tcase map[any]any:\n\t\t\tvals = append(vals, getEnvVars(fmt.Sprintf(\"%s_%v\", prefix, key), v)...)\n\t\tcase []any:\n\t\t\tbuilder := strings.Builder{}\n\t\t\tfor i, s := range v {\n\t\t\t\tswitch s := s.(type) {\n\t\t\t\tcase map[any]any:\n\t\t\t\t\t// descend into slices of objects\n\t\t\t\t\tvals = append(vals, getEnvVars(fmt.Sprintf(\"%s_%v\", prefix, key), s)...)\n\t\t\t\t\tcontinue OUTER\n\t\t\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\t\t\tbuilder.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\"%v\", s))\n\t\t\t\t\tif i < len(v)-1 {\n\t\t\t\t\t\tbuilder.WriteByte(' ')\n\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tvals = append(vals, [2]string{\n\t\t\t\tfmt.Sprintf(\"%s_%s\", strings.ToUpper(prefix), strings.ToUpper(fmt.Sprintf(\"%v\", key))),\n\t\t\t\tbuilder.String(),\n\t\t\t})\n\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\tvals = append(vals, [2]string{\n\t\t\t\tfmt.Sprintf(\"%s_%s\", strings.ToUpper(prefix), strings.ToUpper(fmt.Sprintf(\"%v\", key))),\n\t\t\t\tfmt.Sprintf(\"%v\", value),\n\t\t\t})\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn vals\n}\n\nfunc TestMarshalYAML(t *testing.T) {\n\ttests := []struct {\n\t\tname    string\n\t\tpath    string\n\t\twantErr error\n\t\tcfg     func() *Config\n\t}{\n\t\t{\n\t\t\tname: tt.wantErr\n\n\t\t\texpected, err := os.ReadFile(tt.path)\n\t\t\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\t\t\tout, err := yaml.Marshal(tt.cfg())\n\t\t\tif wantErr != nil {\n\t\t\t\tt.Log(err)\n\t\t\t\tmatch := false\n\t\t\t\tif errors.Is(err, wantErr) {\n\t\t\t\t\tmatch = true\n\t\t\t\t} else if err.Error() == wantErr.Error() {\n\t\t\t\t\tmatch = true\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\trequire.True(t, match, \"expected be snake_case but is '%s'\", tName, fieldName, yamlTag)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// recursively validate the struct tags for all sub-structs.\n\t\tif fieldType.Type.Kind() == reflect.Struct {\n\t\t\tvalidateStructTags(t, getStructTags(fieldType.Type), fieldType.Type)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc isCamelCase(s string) bool {\n\treturn s == strcase.ToLowerCamel(s)\n}\n\nfunc isSnakeCase(s \"\" {\n\t\t\t\tfieldTags[tag] = tagValue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\ttags[fieldName] = fieldTags\n\t}\n\n\treturn tags\n}\n\nfunc TestLicenseConfig_validate(t *testing.T) {\n\ttests := []struct
